		window.showWelcomeAd = false;

  <script>
   (function($){ // anon function
		var debug = false;
		
		window.welcomeId = 'bic';
		if (debug) console.log("Welcome Id: "+welcomeId);
		welcomeId += welcomeId ? '_' : '';
		var waDomain = ".bankinvestmentconsultant.com";
				
		// General Cookie functions
		setCookie = function(cookieName, cookieValue, expire) {
			if (expire) {
				var expires = "; expires=" + expire.toGMTString();
			}
			else var expires = "";
			document.cookie = cookieName + "=" +  escape(cookieValue) + "; domain=" + escape(waDomain) + expires + "; path=/";
		}
		
		getCookie = function(cookieName) {
			var i,x,y,ARRcookies=document.cookie.split(";");
			for (i=0;i&lt;ARRcookies.length;i++) {
				x=ARRcookies[i].substr(0,ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));
				y=ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=")+1);
				x=x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
				if (x==cookieName) {
					return unescape(y);
				}
			}
			return null;
		}
	
		function deleteCookie (name) {
			var exp = new Date();
			exp.setTime (exp.getTime() - 1);
			var cval = getCookie (name);
			document.cookie = name + "=" + cval + "; expires=" + exp.toGMTString();
		}
		// END - General Cookie functions

		if (debug) console.log('function loaded and called.');

		// check if the welcome ad should fire
		var userAgent = navigator.userAgent;
		if (userAgent.indexOf("Sailthru Content Spider") == -1){
			var now = (new Date()).getTime();
			var interval = (1-0) * 60000;
			var maxCount = 1 - 0;
			var expire = (new Date()).getTime() + (24-0) * 3600000;
			expire = new Date(expire);
			if (getCookie(welcomeId + "wa_first") == null) { // never seen
				setCookie(welcomeId + "wa_first", now, expire);
				setCookie(welcomeId + "wa_last", now, expire);
				setCookie(welcomeId + "wa_count", 1, expire);
				showInterstitial = 'Welcome Ad';
				showWelcomeAd = true;
				if (debug) console.log('NEW. now: '+now+', expire: '+expire+', count: 1');
			} else {
				var count = getCookie(welcomeId + "wa_count") - 0;
				var last_seen = getCookie(welcomeId + "wa_last") - 0;
				if (interval &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; last_seen + interval &lt; now &amp;&amp; count &lt; maxCount) {
					setCookie(welcomeId + "wa_last", now, expire);
					setCookie(welcomeId + "wa_count", count + 1, expire);
					showInterstitial = 'Welcome Ad';
					showWelcomeAd = true;
					if (debug) console.log('now: '+now+', expire: '+expire+', count: '+(count+1)+' of '+maxCount);
				} else if (debug) {
					console.log('now: '+now+', expire: '+expire+', count: '+count+' of '+maxCount+', next: '+(last_seen+interval)+', diff: '+(last_seen+interval-now));
				}
			}
			if (debug) console.log('showInterstitial: '+showInterstitial+', showWelcomeAd: '+showWelcomeAd);
		} // end showWelcomeAd check

		if (showWelcomeAd){
		
			$(function(){ // doc ready
				if (debug) console.log('showing ad');
			
				function goBack(){
					$('.welcome-overlay').hide();
					$('html, body').css({overflow:""});
				}
				
				var timer = 10000;
				var count= timer/1000;
				var timeSpent=0;
				var counter;
				function countdown(){
					timeSpent++;
					if (count-- &lt;= 0) {
						clearInterval(counter);
						ga('send', 'event', 'Overlay Welcome Ad', 'Auto Redirect to Site', {'nonInteraction':1});
						goBack();
						return;
					}
				}
				counter=setInterval(countdown, 1000); //1000 will run it every 1 second

				ga('send', 'event', 'Overlay Welcome Ad', 'Impression', {'nonInteraction':1});
				$('#wait').click(function() {
					clearInterval(counter);
					goBack();
					ga('send', 'event', 'Overlay Welcome Ad', 'Skip Ad', 'Time Spent on Ad',timeSpent, {'nonInteraction':1});
				});
								setTimeout(function(){$('#wait').show();},1500);
							}); // end doc ready
		} // end if showWelcomeAd		

	})(jQuery);
  </script>
